-- 3. Develop the Base SALES report of your database (5%)
/*
Customer data: customer number, last name, full name (concatenation of custNo, first name, and and last name), gender, city, state
*/
select customer_no, lname ,customer_no|| ' '|| fname|| ' '|| lname as fullname, gender,city,state from customer;

-- 2
/*
Customer orders: order number, date, product number, product name, quantity, unit price, sub-total, tax (use customer city/state as the base for tax - you can use the tax table in OES database)
*/
SELECT o.order_no,o.order_date,p.product_no,p.prod_name,ol.qty,p.unit_price,o.subtotal,tax_rate
from product p join orderline ol 
on ol.product_no=p.product_no
join orders o
on ol.order_no=o.order_no
join customer c
on c.customer_no=o.customer_no
join tax t
on t.state=c.state

--3.Employee data: employee number, last name, full name (concatenation of first name, and last name), gender, city, state, position title, commission
select * from employee;
select employee_no,fname ||' '||lname as fullname,gender,city,state,ep.description,commission from employee e
JOIN employee_position ep
on e.position=ep.position;
